FROM (
    SELECT c.complaint_id, c.category_id, c.closed_at, c.complaint_description, c.complaint_title, c.created_at, c.current_handler_employee_id, c.escalation_due_at, c.escalation_level, c.priority_id, c.raised_by_employee_id, c.reopened_count, c.resolved_at, c.status_id, c.updated_at
    FROM complaints AS c
    WHERE c.current_handler_employee_id = @employeeId AND c.status_id IN (2, 3, 4)
    ORDER BY c.escalation_due_at
    LIMIT @p2 OFFSET @p
) AS c1
INNER JOIN complaint_statuses AS c0 ON c1.status_id = c0.status_id
INNER JOIN priorities AS p ON c1.priority_id = p.priority_id
INNER JOIN categories AS c2 ON c1.category_id = c2.category_id
INNER JOIN departments AS d ON c2.department_id = d.department_id
INNER JOIN employees AS e ON c1.raised_by_employee_id = e.employee_id
LEFT JOIN employees AS e0 ON c1.current_handler_employee_id = e0.employee_id
ORDER BY c1.escalation_due_at

    LEFT JOIN employees AS e0 ON c.current_handler_employee_id = e0.employee_id
    WHERE c.complaint_id = @id
    LIMIT 1
) AS s
LEFT JOIN complaint_attachments AS c2 ON s.complaint_id = c2.complaint_id
ORDER BY s.complaint_id, s.status_id0, s.priority_id0, s.category_id0, s.department_id0, s.employee_id, s.employee_id0

SELECT e0.employee_id, e0.created_at, e0.department_id, e0.email, e0.employee_name, e0.is_active, e0.mobile_number, e0.password_hash, e0.role_id, e0.updated_at, r.role_id, r.created_at, r.role_name, d.department_id, d.created_at, d.department_head_employee_id, d.department_name, d.is_active, d.updated_at
FROM (
    SELECT e.employee_id, e.created_at, e.department_id, e.email, e.employee_name, e.is_active, e.mobile_number, e.password_hash, e.role_id, e.updated_at
    FROM employees AS e
    ORDER BY e.employee_id

) AS e0

    LIMIT @p1 OFFSET @p
) AS r0
INNER JOIN employees AS e ON r0.employee_id = e.employee_id
INNER JOIN roles AS r1 ON r0.current_role_id = r1.role_id
INNER JOIN roles AS r2 ON r0.requested_role_id = r2.role_id
INNER JOIN request_statuses AS r3 ON r0.request_status_id = r3.request_status_id
LEFT JOIN employees AS e0 ON r0.reviewed_by = e0.employee_id
ORDER BY r0.created_at DESC
